## Workspace package summaries
### apps/api/package.json
- Name: @easyfinderai/api
- Version: 0.0.0
- Scripts:
  - build: tsc -p tsconfig.json
  - dev: pnpm --filter @easyfinderai/shared build && tsx watch src/index.ts
  - lint: eslint -c ../../eslint.config.js src tests --ext .ts
  - promote-admin: tsx scripts/promote-admin.ts
  - test: vitest run
  - typecheck: tsc -p tsconfig.test.json --noEmit
- Dependencies:

openapi: 3.0.3
info:
  title: EasyFinder API
  version: 1.1.0
  description: >
    EasyFinder API contract aligned to currently implemented routes in apps/api.
    Updated to include IronPlanet scraping ingestion and correct NDA/Auth behaviors.

servers:
  - url: https://easyfinder.fly.dev
    description: Production
  - url: http://localhost:8080
    description: Local

tags:
  - name: System
  - name: Auth
  - name: Listings
  - name: Demo Listings
  - name: Scoring
  - name: Watchlist
  - name: Inquiries
  - name: Offers
  - name: Seller
  - name: Admin
  - name: Me
  - name: NDA
  - name: Billing
  - name: Scrapers

paths:
  /health:
    get:
      tags: [System]
      summary: Root health check
      responses:
        "200":
          description: Service status
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                type: object
                required: [ok, demoMode, billingEnabled]
                properties:
                  ok: { type: boolean }
                  demoMode: { type: boolean }
                  billingEnabled: { type: boolean }

  /ready:
    get:
      tags: [System]
      summary: Readiness probe
      responses:
        "200":
          description: Readiness state
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                type: object
                required: [ready]
                properties:
                  ready: { type: boolean }

              schema:
                type: object
                required: [ok]

          description: Demo listing detail
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: "#/components/schemas/ListingResponse"
        "404":
          $ref: "#/components/responses/NotFoundError"

  /api/listings:

      summary: Get ranked live listings
      security:

      responses:
        "200":
          description: Live listing array
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: "#/components/schemas/ListingsResponse"
        "401": { $ref: "#/components/responses/UnauthorizedError" }
        "402": { $ref: "#/components/responses/PaymentRequiredError" }
        "403": { $ref: "#/components/responses/NdaRequiredError" }
        "503": { $ref: "#/components/responses/DemoModeActiveError" }
    post:
      tags: [Listings]
      summary: Create listing (not implemented)
      security:
        - bearerAuth: []
      responses:
        "401": { $ref: "#/components/responses/UnauthorizedError" }
        "403":
          description: NDA required or writes disabled in demo mode
          content:
            application/json:
              schema: { $ref: "#/components/schemas/ErrorEnvelope" }
        "501":
          description: Not implemented
          content:
            application/json:
              schema: { $ref: "#/components/schemas/ErrorEnvelope" }
    put:
      tags: [Listings]
      summary: Update listing (not implemented)

        - bearerAuth: []

  /api/listings/{id}:
    get:
      tags: [Listings]

      security:
        - bearerAuth: []
      parameters:
        - $ref: "#/components/parameters/ListingId"
      responses:
        "200":
          description: Live listing detail
          content:

        "503": { $ref: "#/components/responses/DemoModeActiveError" }

  /api/scrape/ironplanet:
    get:
      tags: [Scrapers]
      summary: Scrape IronPlanet search results and upsert into live listings
      description: >
        Scrapes an IronPlanet search results page (url query param), extracts listings,
        and upserts them into MongoDB. Writes are blocked when DEMO_MODE is enabled.
      parameters:
        - in: query
          name: url
          required: true
          schema:
            type: string
          description: URL-encoded IronPlanet search URL to scrape.
      responses:
        "200":
          description: Scrape + upsert summary
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: "#/components/schemas/ScrapeIronPlanetResponse"
        "400":
          description: Invalid request (missing/invalid url)
          content:
            application/json:
              schema: { $ref: "#/components/schemas/ErrorEnvelope" }
        "403":
          description: Writes disabled in demo mode
          content:
            application/json:
              schema: { $ref: "#/components/schemas/ErrorEnvelope" }
        "500":
          description: Scrape failure
          content:
            application/json:
              schema: { $ref: "#/components/schemas/ErrorEnvelope" }

  /api/scoring-configs:

                $ref: "#/components/schemas/ScoringConfigEnvelope"

## File: README.md
```
# EasyFinder

Intelligent equipment discovery and scoring in a pnpm monorepo.

## What this repo contains

- **`apps/api`**: Fastify API for listings, auth, scoring config, seller/admin workflows, and billing gates.
- **`apps/web`**: Vite + React frontend.
- **`packages/shared`**: shared domain types/utilities consumed by API and web.

## Documentation Index

- Product vision + acquisition strategy: `docs/product/PRODUCT_VISION.md`
- Scoring model semantics: `docs/product/SCORING_MODEL.md`
- Engineering/system overview (including admin, frontend contract, billing/webhook notes): `docs/engineering/SYSTEM_OVERVIEW.md`
- AI/dev invariants only: `docs/engineering/AI_DEV_CONTEXT.md`
- API contract (canonical): `openapi.yml`

## Local development

### Prerequisites

- Node.js 20.x
- pnpm 9.6.0+

### Environment setup

```bash
cp apps/api/.env.example apps/api/.env
cp apps/web/.env.example apps/web/.env
```

Notes:
- `apps/api/.env` must be configured with required backend secrets/settings.
- `apps/web/.env` should set `VITE_API_BASE_URL`.

### Frontend API base URL contract

Use host-only API origin without `/api`:

- Local: `VITE_API_BASE_URL=http://127.0.0.1:8080`
- Production example: `VITE_API_BASE_URL=https://easyfinder.fly.dev`

The web client normalizes paths and adds `/api` as needed.

### Install, run, verify

```bash
pnpm install
pnpm dev
```

Common verification:

```bash
pnpm -w lint
pnpm -w typecheck
pnpm -w test
pnpm -w build
```

## OpenAPI workflow

`openapi.yml` is the single API source of truth.

When API contract changes:

1. Update `openapi.yml`.
2. Regenerate web types:
   ```bash
   pnpm -w openapi:types
   ```
3. Commit the generated file changes together.

## Safety checklist before merge/deploy

- Import shared modules only through `@easyfinderai/shared` (no deep imports from `packages/shared/src`).
- Keep Docker build sequence deterministic (shared build before dependent app builds).
- Preserve Fly runtime assumptions unless intentionally changing infra:
  - API port `8080`
  - health endpoint available
  - runtime entry `node dist/index.js`
- Run full workspace gates:
  - `pnpm -w lint`
  - `pnpm -w typecheck`
  - `pnpm -w test`
  - `pnpm -w build`

## Admin bootstrap / promote flow

To safely promote an existing user to `admin` without editing Mongo manually, run the API helper with `MONGO_URL` and `DB_NAME` set in `apps/api/.env`: `pnpm --filter @easyfinderai/api promote-admin -- --email fernandogarciarodriguez78@gmail.com`; in production it is blocked unless you intentionally pass `--allow-production` (`pnpm --filter @easyfinderai/api promote-admin -- --email fernandogarciarodriguez78@gmail.com --allow-production`), and the command prints email searched, user id, previous role â†’ new role, and a final `DONE`/`NOOP` status.
```

## File: .easyfinder-context.md
```
# Deprecated Context Path

This legacy file has been consolidated.

Use `docs/engineering/AI_DEV_CONTEXT.md` for AI/dev rules and invariants, and use the canonical docs index in `README.md` for product/engineering references.
```

- Updated image serving architecture

- Converted listing grid from 2 → 4 columns
